### Analysis:
- **DoS (Denial of Service)**: An attack meant to shut down a machine or network, making it inaccessible to its intended users. DoS attacks accomplish this by flooding the target with traffic or sending it information that triggers a crash.
- **DDoS (Distributed Denial of Service)**: Similar to DoS but involves multiple compromised computer systems attacking a target, such as a server, website, or other network resource, and causing a denial of service for users of the targeted resource.

### Conclusion:

Therefore, the final classification is **DDoS-UDP_Flood**.

### Analysis:
- **DoS (Denial of Service)**: An attack meant to shut down a machine or network, making it inaccessible to its intended users. DoS attacks accomplish this by flooding the target with traffic or sending it information that triggers a crash.
- **DDoS (Distributed Denial of Service)**: Similar to DoS but involves multiple compromised computer systems attacking a target, such as a server, website, or other network resource, and causing a denial of service for users of the targeted resource.
